***lomp.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lomp.html>lomp</a> (12154)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Uncertain. Perhaps from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lomp.html>lomp</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rag</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:lomp.html>lomp</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rude</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">German Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de">Lump</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bounder; cad</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Lump</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rogue; cad</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lomp.html>lomp</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lomper.html>lomper</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">lompst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>coarse; rude; surly; boorish; unrefined; uncouth; unsophisticated; unmannered
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeg.html>Zeg</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lompe.html>lompe</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:boer.html>boer</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:staat.html>staat</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:trapt.html>trapt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eens.html>eens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uw.html>uw</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eigen.html>eigen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tenen.html>tenen</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:hey.html>Hey</a>, unmannered <a href = vnd.unilang:boor.html>boor</a>, step on your own <a href = vnd.unilang:toes.html>toes</a>, will you!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly southern</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dumb
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>Hoe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunt.html>kunt</a> ge <a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lomp.html>lomp</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weten.html>weten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoeveel.html>hoeveel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>twee</a> plus <a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>twee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>?!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">How can you be so <b>dumb</b> not knowing how much <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> two plus two?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lomperd.html>lomperd</a> (39260)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lomp.html>lomp</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-erd</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lomperd.html>lomperd</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lomperds.html>lomperds</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lomperd.html>lomperdje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A crude or churlish person, a lummox, a <a href = vnd.unilang:boor.html>boor</a>.</li></ol>

***lonen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lonen.html>lonen</a> (18403)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lônen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*lōnon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*launōn</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:loon.html>loon</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lonen.html>lonen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be rewarding, to pay, to be profitable
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:misdaad.html>Misdaad</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:loont.html>loont</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Crime doesn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <b>pay</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:belonen.html>belonen</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lont.html>lont</a> (11864)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lont.html>lont</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lonten.html>lonten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lontje.html>lontje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">fuse</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">for explosive device</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

***loodrecht.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:loodrecht.html>loodrecht</a> (53965)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lood.html>lood</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">plumb <a href = vnd.unilang:bob.html>bob</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:recht.html>recht</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">straight</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Purism introduced by <a href = vnd.unilang:simon.html>Simon</a> Stevin in the 16th century to replace the Dutch word <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">perpendiculair</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">perpendicular</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> which <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a borrowing from Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">perpendiculum</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:loodrecht.html>loodrecht</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:loodrecht.html>loodrechter</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">loodrechtst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>perpendicular, orthogonal</li>
<li>vertical</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">perpendicular</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">orthogonaal</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:loods.html>loods</a> (12290)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Back-formation from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">loodsman</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lootsman</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">lodesman</i> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lodesman</i>).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:loods.html>loods</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:loodsen.html>loodsen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:loods.html>loodsje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">navigation</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pilot, expert who helps navigate to the harbor or coast</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">zoology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pilot fish</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> guide</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:loonlijst.html>loonlijst</a> (14935)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:loon.html>loon</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pay, wages</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijst.html>lijst</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">list</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***loopafstand.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:loopafstand.html>loopafstand</a> (45143)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lopen.html>lopen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afstand.html>afstand</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:loopafstand.html>loopafstand</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:loopafstand.html>loopafstanden</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> walking distance <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">distance of a comfortable walk</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span> <span class="defdate">[from 20th c.]</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the distance one <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> to cover by walking, especially of a pedestrian route <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. in sporting events or in recreational facilities</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="defdate">[from early 20th c.]</span></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:loos.html>loos</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*lōs</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lausaz</i>.

***lopen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lopen.html>lopen</a> (438)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lôpen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*lōpan</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*loupan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*hlaupan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hlaupaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to run</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lopen.html>lopen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgium" class="extiw" title="w:Belgium">Belgium</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to run, go fast on one's own <a href = vnd.unilang:legs.html>legs</a>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stad.html>stad</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gelopen.html>gelopen</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ran.html>ran</a></b> to the city.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgium" class="extiw" title="w:Belgium">Belgium</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to run, cover distance, follow a track etc.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gelopen.html>gelopen</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> a lot of <b>running</b> there.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be open, current, activated</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lose liquid: drip, gush, leak
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lekken.html>lekken</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:druppen.html>druppen</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Forms a continuous aspect. Although it <a href = vnd.unilang:carries.html>carries</a> an implication of walking, this <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> vague and not emphasized.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:loop.html>loop</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>jij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">What <b>are</b> you doing there?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>In Flanders, the word usually means "to run", while in the Netherlands it usually means "to walk". An identical phrase will thus be interpreted differently depending on the area where the speaker <a href = vnd.unilang:comes.html>comes</a> from. In Netherlands, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rennen.html>rennen</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the common word for <i>run</i>.
</p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">loope</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lopin</i> (perhaps cognate with French), presumably a diminutive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:loop.html>loop</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">jump</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">leap</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lopen.html>lopen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="gender incomplete">?</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:loopje.html>loopje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A dry measure of content</li>

***loper.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:loper.html>loper</a> (8754)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lopere</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lopen.html>lopen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:loper.html>loper</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lopers.html>lopers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:loper.html>lopertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>runner
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">hardloper</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:renner.html>renner</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>somebody who walks</li>
<li>a carpet
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:rode.html>rode</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:loper.html>loper</a></i>  |  red carpet</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chess</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bishop.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:raadsheer.html>raadsheer</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>master key
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">moedersleutel</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>message runner, messager who <a href = vnd.unilang:runs.html>runs</a> on foot</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">shoot</span> from the roots of a plant
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitloper.html>uitloper</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***loris.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:loris.html>loris</a> (91078)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:loris.html>loris</a></i>, reportedly from obsolete Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">loeris</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">simpleton</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:loris.html>loris</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">lorises</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any of several small, slow-moving primates, of the family Lorisidae, found in India and southeast Asia.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:los.html>los</a> (503)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:los.html>los</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:los.html>los</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lusaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:los.html>los</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:losser.html>losser</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:los.html>los</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>lost</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>loose</li>
<li>separate</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_4">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:los.html>los</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:los.html>los</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*luhsuz</i>, perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*lewk-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">light, to shine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stratum_(linguistics)" class="extiw" title="w:Stratum (linguistics)">substrate</a></span> language.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-5"> | 1 | </a></sup> Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">lohs</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">luhs</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">lox</i>, from a similar Germanic form also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">lodjur</i>. Cognates outside Germanic include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">λύγξ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lúnx</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">lūšis</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">роусь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rusĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Irish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Irish">Old Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sga">lug</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Classical_Armenian" class="extiw" title="w:Classical Armenian">Old Armenian</a></span> <i class="Armn mention" lang="xcl">լուսանունք</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="xcl-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lusanunkʿ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***lossen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lossen.html>lossen</a> (2498)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Derived from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:los.html>los</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rid; free</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">löschen</i> (etymology 2).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lossen.html>lossen</a></strong>
</p>

<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span></span>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:loupe.html>loupe</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sapphire lens, imperfect gem, mass of hot metal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*luppa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">something pendulous</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lubbǭ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">that which hangs or dangles</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lub-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to peel, hang</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*lep-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to peel, skin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span></span> dialectal (Meuse-Rhenish) <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">luppe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">piece</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span></span> and <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lobbe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dangling part</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saterland_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Saterland Frisian language">Saterland Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq">lobbe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hanging lump of flesh</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hanging lip, ruffle or sleeve</span><span More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">lobe</span>.

***louter.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:louter.html>louter</a> (13470)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:louter.html>louter</a></i>, variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">luyter</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">lûter</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">lutter</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*lūtir</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">luttir</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hlūtraz</i>. The <i>-ou-</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> probably due to influence by late <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">lauter</i>, older <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">lūter</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">hlūter</i>, from the same Germanic source. Compare modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">lauter</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:louter.html>louter</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:louter.html>louterder</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">louterst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inflected</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pure
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:louter.html>louterste</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:goud.html>goud</a></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the <b>purest</b> gold</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">invariable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a lot of; a bunch of
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:louter.html>louter</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:leugens.html>leugens</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It’s <b>a bunch of</b> lies.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>Er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:louter.html>louter</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:regels.html>regels</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:volgen.html>volgen</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">There are <b>a lot of</b> rules <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> must follow.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Sense 2 <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> originally a use of the adverb “purely” and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> sometimes still interpretable as such. In the second example sentence, however, this <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> clearly not the case.</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:louter.html>louter</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>purely</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:louter.html>louter</a></b>

<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:eerste.html>eerste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:persoon.html>persoon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:enkelvoud.html>enkelvoud</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tegenwoordige.html>tegenwoordige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> louteren<br />

***loven.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:loven.html>loven</a> (20286)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:loven.html>loven</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">lovon</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to praise, to sing psalms</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lubōną</i>.
</p>
